I've always been interested in trying Jerusalem Grill, or I stopped by their brunch buffet (11 AM to 3 PM) for a wonderful meal. For only $13.99, you get quite a few items that are really sure to whet your appetite. The chicken shawarma was amazing, nicely spiced to perfection and went well with the jasmine rice and bread. Give Jerusalem Grill a try!< /Text>

<user_name>shiva sharma<//user_name>< Date>

<Rating>2<//Rating><review>Downgrading from 4 to 2 stars.

First the pros; the chicken shawarma is nicely seasoned and one of the better ones in the bay area. Their hummus is also pretty good.

The cons overshadow the pros though and I have no interest in wasting time here anymore.

Service is extremely slow regardless of when you come in. I've been the first customer through the door on weekdays and have had to wait 30 mins + to get my meal because they seem to prioritize any phone orders/catering and they simply don't have the manpower to deal with that. They'll have the same cashier running back and forth between prepping bags for to go orders and taking your order (while you're waiting in front of the cash register) in a very disorganized fashion. Happened about 3 times before I decided it's not worth coming here on weekdays because it really eats up your lunch hour.

On weekends they have a "brunch" buffet. In the past they've always allowed customers to choose between the buffet or ordering off the menu. The menu items are of slightly better quality usually; the chicken in the buffet is usually dry and the other meat option varies - can be fish or beef etc, and if you don't eat beef then you'd want to order off the regular menu. This last weekend we arrived at 11:55 am for lunch. This was 25 mins past their opening time of 11:30. First they told us we couldn't order off the regular menu. No idea if this is a new policy or they just decided on the spot to not accommodate us. The only option was to order the buffet, but their buffet wasn't ready (aside from the hummus and salad station).
So 25 mins after opening they're still not ready for buffet service, yet they'll give no option besides the buffet to customers? That's just laughably bad service.

They don't seem to care about their business, so why should I bother coming here again.<//review><Pics>None< /Pics><response>None<//response>< gmapID>
0x808e3527d3f00933:0xa77e09364a19edf0< /gmapID>

< Review>
I went there before one week to try their Mediterranean food. I'm an Arab person so it's easy to know the good from the bad Mediterranean food. Overall I liked the place. Clean area and the service is great. The owner is such a friendly and awesome man. Loved their chicken shawarma (just like the one I used to eat back home). I didn't like their tabula salad, the bulgur was too much. The Kanufa is a must try, fresh and yummy (just like the Turkish way). Will go there again.</Review>

<review>Getting your car serviced is like going to the dentist or the doctors- you dread going and keep your fingers crossed that there aren't any major discoveries. However, I've been to A1 on three separate occasions now, and I would have to say, that, overall, it's a pretty pleasant experience. Brad, the owner, is genuinely a honest, funny, and patient guy who does such a great job at explaining any work that needs to be done. Although during my most recent visit, it was discovered that I needed some extra work done, he explained to me that it didn't need to be done right away as it was not critical to the car being operational. Most mechanics won't tell you that. They are after your money. Brad is different. He understands that his customers have different needs and he does a great job of explaining what the options are. One of my favorite things about coming to A1 is the fact that whenever there's something that needs to be worked on, Brad will have one of the mechanics walk me over to the car, show me the item, and educate me if it's something I am not too familiar with. Today, his son Justin, worked on my car. He did a great job and was always pleasant in demeanor. He also took the time to explain an issue I was having with my car after he did some discovery work.
In general, I think if you dread taking your car to the shop it's usually a sign that you don't have a lot of trust in your mechanic. After my 3rd visit here, I can confidently say that I don't dread having A1 work on my car. I already know what to expect- honest work, fair prices,  great employees, Brad's great sense of humor, and being treated like a valued customer. If you're looking for a new place that you can trust, A1 is it!< /review>< pictures>

< Review>
